The Late Match King's Numerous Crimes During His Lifetime 99

Another Rumor About the Reason for His Suicide

Stockholm, 16th (National News Agency dispatch). Regarding the various malfeasance of Match King Kreuger during his lifetime, it is now reported that according to investigations, Kreuger had been engaging in various forgery activities since as early as 1925, and his crimes were so numerous that even if his business was going well, he would not be able to escape the net. The most recent new discovery is the contract that Kreuger's Continental Investment Corporation signed with former Spanish leader Rivera in 1925. According to the contract, Kreuger's Continental Investment Corporation lent the Spanish government 180 million pesetas (Spanish currency) with an annual interest rate of 1.8%, in exchange for the monopoly on match manufacturing in Spain. It has now been discovered that this contract was also forged, and there are other astonishing discoveries. The Kreuger case investigation committee has dispatched specialists to Paris to obtain Rivera's signature sample. However, according to the three people who have been arrested in connection with the Kreuger case, Kreuger fabricated numerous documents during his lifetime, too numerous to mention. This is just one example.

Berlin, 16th (Havas dispatch). After the exposure of the case of the Swedish Match King Kreuger forging documents during his lifetime, the German financial world has had a very negative impression. Those who once recognized Kreuger as a perfect person in the business world now denounce him as an unprecedented fraudster. Outside reports say that the entanglement between Kreuger and Morgan Bank in New York was the direct cause of his suicide. Previously, Morgan Bank had agreed to lend Kreuger 3 million US dollars, but Kreuger needed to use the shares of International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation as collateral. However, after Kreuger borrowed the money, he did not hand over the shares. Morgan Bank then ordered Kreuger to hand them over immediately, or return the money. Kreuger then left the United States for France, still hoping to raise 3 million US dollars in Paris to save the situation. After arriving in the French capital, he begged for help in vain, and in despair, he committed suicide. It is also rumored that Kreuger's forged Italian bonds were about to be handed over to the Italian government.

Important News

The League of Nations Investigation Team Conducts Investigation Work in Peiping 102

Repeated Meetings with Zhang Xueliang, Rong Zhen, and Others

Detailed Study of the South Manchuria Railway Parallel Line Issue

Peiping Correspondence. The League of Nations Investigation Team has been conducting various investigation work in Peiping for several days. A brief account is as follows:

Meeting with Rong Zhen and Wang Yizhe. At the reception tea party on the evening of their arrival in Peiping, Sir Lytton and others from the League of Nations Investigation Team met with Rong Zhen, the former Chief of Staff of the Northeast Border Defense Command, and inquired about Rong's account of the September 18th Incident witnessed in Shenyang. Due to time constraints, they only discussed the general outline. At 10:30 a.m. on the 13th, Lytton and the other five commissioners formally received Rong and Wang Yizhe, the commander of the 7th Brigade of the Northeast Army, at the Beijing Hotel, and discussed the situation in detail. Wang was stationed in Beidaying at the beginning of the Shenyang Incident, and the Japanese army on the South Manchuria Railway opened fire to provoke, and his troops bore the brunt. Wang reported the truth one by one. Rong also stated that the reason for not resisting the Japanese army's unprovoked provocations in Shenyang was to believe that the League of Nations would be able to sanction Japan's atrocities, so as to avoid the devastation of the region and the suffering of foreign nationals. Finally, Lytton asked Rong and Wang to prepare a written account of the September 18th Incident and submit it to the team for reference during the investigation and report to the League of Nations. The conversation lasted about two hours before Rong and Wang bid farewell.

Discussing the Parallel Line Issue. At 3:00 p.m. on the 13th, the investigation team met with Chinese representative Gu Weijun and Japanese representative Yoshida. During the meeting, the issues of leaving the customs and the parallel lines of the South Manchuria Railway were discussed in detail. Yoshida had a heated argument with Gu on the spot. Regarding the matter of leaving the customs, Yoshida said that the Japanese side welcomed the investigation team leaving the customs, but regarding the issue of Gu Weijun's accompanying them, Yoshida repeated the instructions of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, nothing more than promising to provide protection within the possible scope. The opinions of the commissioners of the investigation team were that if they could not be fully responsible for Gu's protection, they would not leave the customs. Regarding the South Manchuria Railway parallel line issue, Yoshida stated that China's construction of parallel railways violated the Sino-Japanese treaty. Gu Weijun then pointed out that although the articles in the annex to a certain Sino-Japanese treaty stipulated that railways could not be built within 100 Chinese li of the South Manchuria Railway, the Datong Railway currently being built by China was more than 200 Chinese li away from the South Manchuria Railway, which did not violate the treaty provisions, and that the treaty had not been formally signed by the Chinese side. Yoshida was speechless and the debate stopped. Immediately afterwards, the commissioners and Gu and the Secretary-General Haas went to Shuncheng Wangfu at around 4 o'clock to hold the second talk with Zhang Xueliang. Zhang Zuoxiang, Wan Fulin, Mi Chunlin, Rong Zhen, and other former senior officials from the Northeast all attended, but the Japanese representatives did not participate. They discussed various Northeast issues. Lytton inquired in detail about the South Manchuria Railway parallel line issue. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 p.m. Overall, the main points of the investigation team's research concentrated on the South Manchuria parallel line issue. It was decided that the third meeting would continue at 4:00 p.m. on the 14th. In addition to the people who participated on the 13th, Liu Zhe and Wang Yizhe also joined. It is said that after the third meeting, it was decided that no more meetings would be held and that all actual materials would be sorted out. On the morning of the 14th, the investigation team also held a routine meeting to discuss and decide on the itinerary for the first trip to the Eastern Provinces.

Receiving Representatives of the People. The investigation team began receiving representatives of various groups from the 12th. That afternoon, they received Xiong Xiling, Chen Zhenxian, Ye Shuheng, Liao Shigong, Wang Wenxian, and others, representatives of the Chinese League of Nations Association. First, Xiong and others presented a written report, including a welcome letter, a booklet on the Sino-Japanese conflict, and a memorandum. Then, they talked and raised various important issues, asking the team to pay attention. Lytton expressed his satisfaction.

Our Country Delivers Memorandum. The memorandum delivered by our country to the League of Nations Investigation Team includes more than a hundred pending cases, such as Sino-Japanese negotiations on roads and mines in the Northeast, the Wanbaoshan Incident, and anti-Chinese sentiment among Koreans, all of which are explained in detail. This memorandum has been drafted and completed, and Chinese representative Gu Weijun divided it into several major parts and handed it to Lytton. As of the 12th, only the section on the Eastern Province Railway parallel line issue had not yet been delivered. It is expected that Gu will present it in person within a day or two for reference when going to the Northeast for investigation in the future.

Decision to Reject the Puppet State's Reception. The League of Nations Investigation Team decided to leave the customs on a special train of the Beining Railway. The fact that Chinese representative Xian Weijun accompanied them did not change due to the puppet state's telegram of rejection. After the investigation team arrives in the Northeast, it will immediately engage in practical investigation work. Regarding the so-called Manchurian State's reception, because the world's countries have not recognized the "Manchurian State," it was decided to reject it. However, the investigation team can accept the reception from the Japanese Kwantung Army. Because the team is not accepting the puppet state's reception, the Beining Railway special train has begun to be renovated, including bathrooms, sanatoriums, cold storage rooms, laundry rooms, etc., which were not previously prepared, for the team's long-term use after leaving the customs. Also, the Deputy Secretary-General of the Investigation Team, Berridge, met with various reporters at the Beijing Hotel at 6:30 p.m. on the 13th. During the conversation, a Japanese reporter raised several absurd questions, asking what attitude the investigation team would take when the Manchurian State held a banquet. Berridge replied, "For example, in ordinary social situations, if a gentleman invites guests, we will of course participate. If a non-gentleman invites guests, we may not attend." The Japanese reporter also said that the Manchurian State rejected Gu Weijun's entry because Gu had plans to hinder the new country. Berridge only shook his head and smiled without saying anything. (14th)

The Japanese Army's Invasion of Mongolia 104

Major Matsui and Major Iwai Were Killed by Mongolian Soldiers

The Purpose of Invading Mongolia Was to Incite Various Princes to Become Independent

Dalian Correspondence. Since Japan's secret exploration of Mongolia by Nakamaru Shintaro failed last year, it has never slackened its work on spying on Mongolia. In February of this year, the Japanese army again invaded Mongolia. However, Mongolia is located in a remote border area, and news is scarce, so the Chinese people have not heard the details of the incident for several months. It has been investigated that the leader of this invasion of Mongolia was Colonel Matsui Seisuke. Matsui was 55 years old. Six years ago, he was the artillery commander of the Japanese 9th Division. Afterwards, he resigned and served exclusively as an army detective spying on Mongolia. Because he is the maternal uncle of Kawashima Yoshiko (daughter of Prince Gong), he has always been in contact with the princes and leaders of various Mongolian banners. In recent years, he has traveled between Qinghai and Shenyang a total of three times and is a famous Mongolian expert in Japan. When Zhang Zuolin was alive, he served as an advisor to the Marshal's Mansion. After the September 18th Incident last year, he recruited hundreds of bandits in Tongliao and other places to form an army to enter Mongolia, appointing three army commanders and calling himself commander-in-chief, under the control of the Japanese Kwantung Army stationed in Shenyang. The Kwantung Army also provided them with weapons and ammunition. Matsui then advanced step by step into Mongolia. On February 25, they arrived at Linxi County, which belonged to Rehe Province. The Chinese army stationed there actually opened the city and welcomed them with flags. On March 1, they advanced to the Gejiayingzi area, which belonged to Mongolia, when suddenly more than a thousand cavalrymen without flags surrounded Matsui and his subordinates completely. Hundreds of rabble soldiers, along with Matsui and Major Iwai, were all killed. The only one who escaped back to Shenyang was the secretary-general, the traitor Wu Huamin. After Honjo Shigeru received the news, he immediately sent airplanes to Inner Mongolia to demonstrate. According to Wu's account, Matsui's warhorse was shot and killed first during the battle, and then his waist was seriously injured in three places, and he died immediately. Matsui's purpose in entering Mongolia was to incite the independent movement of the Mongolian princes and leaders, so that they could break away from China and form the same situation as the Northeast puppet state.

Enthusiastic Enlistment of Able-Bodied Youths in Guangdong 105

Tan Qixiu's Recruitment Achieves Great Success

Guangzhou Dispatch: Wu Song Fortress Commander Tan Qixiu, since returning to Guangdong, has been actively recruiting supplementary soldiers, preparing for a long-term resistance against Japan. It is reported that Tan plans to first establish a supplementary brigade with the recruited soldiers in Guangdong. Sons and daughters of Guangdong, for the sake of resisting Japan, are all enthusiastically enlisting in the army and sacrificing for the country. The recruitment method involves sending personnel to various subordinate districts to conduct recruitment. Li Jinbo was dispatched to Luoding, Zheng Xingcha to Xinxing and Liangyang, Chen Renyuan to Gaolei, Sun Lanquan to Qinlian, and Zhu Zichao to the five districts of Yulin, Guangxi. After each officer arrived at their destination, the number of enlistees had already reached several thousand. Tan immediately appointed the commanders of each regiment of the supplementary brigade. It is found that Chen Renzhi is the commander of the first regiment, Sun Lanquan is the commander of the second regiment, Xie Zidong is the commander of the third regiment, Zheng Xingcha is the commander of the fourth regiment, and Li Jinbo is the commander of the independent regiment. Those who have already been recruited are issued firearms and training begins. A new recruit training center has been established in Hekou, Sanshui, to concentrate and train new recruits from the Xijiang and Guangxi areas. On the Beijiang side, a brigade headquarters has been established at the Xinjie Station on the Yuehan Railway, and a new recruit transportation office has been established in Huangsha, the provincial capital, and Xu Ji has been appointed to preside over recruitment affairs in Beijiang. Xu Ji was a brigade commander under Xu Chongzhi in the past and has a considerable history in the revolution. This time, he is serving Tan, and most of the soldiers he recruits are also former subordinates of Xu. Currently, the 19th Route Army Headquarters has dispatched more than 20 officers to Guangdong to take charge of the training of new recruits. On the South Road side, the recently recruited new recruits and a portion transferred from Chen Ce's Marine Corps will first form a special service battalion, according to the Class A infantry formation of the army. The battalion is fully staffed with five companies and has received firearms from the 19th Route Army rear office. It is concentrating training in Beihai. On the Guangxi side, recruitment is proceeding with the support of the Guangxi authorities. A regiment of unarmed soldiers of the former subordinates of Hu Ruoping has been recruited, as well as a regiment of unarmed Guizhou soldiers of the former subordinates of Situ Fei. Both regiments have arrived at Hekou, Sanshui and are being concentrated at the new recruit training center.

Firearms will be issued and they will be slightly organized, then they can go to the front lines, because the able-bodied youths of both regiments have long been trained. (April 11th)

Investigation Team Reports on Situation from Western Nanjing (7) 106

Appendix: League of Nations Handling of Sino-Japanese Dispute

Although our country's consistent demand for a deadline for troop withdrawal was abandoned due to opposition from all parties, we still advocate that the future draft resolution should stipulate: (1) The investigation team should have the power to supervise troop withdrawal; (2) When the team arrives at its destination, it should report to the Administrative Yuan on whether Japan has implemented troop withdrawal in accordance with the resolution. Japan, on the other hand, advocates: (1) The investigation team has no right to interfere in the military affairs of both parties; (2) The team should go to the Chinese interior to investigate the situation of boycotting Japanese goods; (3) When the team arrives at the destination, it cannot issue a report proving that Japanese troops have not withdrawn, in order to avoid indirect stipulations for a troop withdrawal deadline; (4) Japan has the right to suppress bandits in the Eastern Provinces.

Among the four points advocated by Japan, the fourth point is the most barbaric and unreasonable, because the right to suppress bandits is the sovereignty of an independent country. Moreover, using bandit suppression as a pretext to advance troops is a common trick of Japan. Now Japan actually asks the Administrative Yuan to grant it the right to suppress bandits in the Eastern Provinces, even the numb and insensitive Administrative Yuan is disgusted by this and therefore flatly refuses. As for the remaining points, after modifying the wording, those agreed to by both parties are retained, and the irreconcilable points are resolved through compromise, with the chairman issuing a separate declaration. Readers will understand when they reach the summary of the resolution and the chairman's declaration.

(3) Meetings on December 9th and 10th and the Situation After the Meetings On December 9th, the Administrative Yuan reconvened a public meeting, and the chairman submitted the draft resolution of the Administrative Yuan and the draft declaration of the chairman for discussion. There were no objections. The chairman asked the Chinese and Japanese representatives to telegram their respective governments for approval. By the next day, December 10th, the Chinese and Japanese representatives had received replies from their respective countries. The chairman then convened a public meeting and submitted the two drafts for a vote. As a result, they were unanimously passed. Before the resolution was submitted for a vote, Briand consulted with the US representative General Stimson and obtained his agreement.

After the resolution was passed, the Japanese representative spoke, saying that Japan supported the draft resolution, but on the condition that it reserved the right to suppress bandits and other troublemakers. The Chinese representative also declared: (1) Reserving all rights granted by international treaties; (2) China recognizes that the chairman's declaration contains the following four principles: (1) Immediately cease military actions; (2) Clear up Japan's occupation of Manchuria within the shortest possible time; (3) All future situations should be continuously reported to the League of Nations by neutral parties; (4) The Administrative Yuan should appoint an investigation team to study the entire situation in Manchuria on the spot. The above four principles are interrelated. Violating one is enough to destroy the others. (3) When the investigation team arrives in Manchuria, if Japanese troops have not withdrawn, the team should immediately report to the League of Nations, and the report should include recommendations. (4) China's right to demand compensation for losses from Japan is not lost due to the current resolution's failure to explicitly stipulate it. (5) Japan cannot use the pretext of unrest in the Eastern Provinces to redeploy troops in the future, because the unrestful environment was created by Japan's use of troops. China absolutely does not recognize the right of foreigners to occupy Chinese territory and maintain law and order on its behalf. (6) The Chinese government may invite neutral personnel to investigate the truth in places designated by it at any time. (7) China's long-standing opposition to the principle of foreign troops stationed on its territory should not be abandoned due to the current resolution. (8) China believes that if Japan creates an independence movement in the Eastern Provinces that harms its territorial and administrative integrity, it will be in violation of the League of Nations resolution.

The British representative stated that although Japan's autonomous bandit suppression is an unavoidable fact, once the original state is restored, this special action should be stopped immediately.

Representatives from other countries also spoke, roughly saying that the Sino-Japanese dispute has been going on for several months, and the current resolution is not a thorough solution, but because the nature of the Manchurian problem is special, its solution should not be a precedent for future international disputes. Representatives from small and weak countries in South America gave even more heartfelt speeches. China's representative Shi also stated that the representatives of various countries clearly know that they are weak and lack courage and dare not resist the violent Japan, and they are also afraid that in future international disputes, someone will follow this precedent and "invite public entry into the urn." Therefore, he specifically declared the special nature of this Sino-Japanese dispute and angrily said in a stern tone that the Chinese government absolutely does not recognize that the effect of international law can only extend to the borders of Manchuria. The conference, which lasted for more than twenty days, thus came to a temporary end.

(4) Study of the Resolution and the Chairman's Declaration The content of the resolution is divided into six items: (1) The Administrative Yuan hereby reiterates the resolution unanimously passed on September 30th. Both China and Japan have the obligation to comply with it. Therefore, we ask the governments of China and Japan to earnestly fulfill it and ensure that Japanese troops withdraw to within the South Manchuria Railway line under the conditions stipulated in the resolution within the shortest possible time. (2) The situation that has occurred since the adjournment of the Administrative Yuan on October 24th has become more serious. Both parties have now agreed to find ways to avoid escalation and to exercise self-restraint to avoid the recurrence of wars and casualties. (3) Please both parties continue to report the latest situation to the Administrative Yuan at any time. (4) Please the governments of other countries report the news sent by their representatives in Manchuria to the Administrative Yuan at any time. (5) In order to assist China and Japan in resolving all outstanding issues, the Administrative Yuan has decided to send a five-member investigation team to Manchuria to study all environments that endanger international relations, peace between China and Japan, or the harmony on which peace between the two countries is based, and report to the Administrative Yuan. It also asks the Chinese and Japanese governments to each send a member to participate in the work of the team and provide the team with all materials. It also declares that the team shall not interfere when China and Japan conduct direct negotiations, and it has no right to interfere in military matters. The Japanese government, because it has the obligation to implement the September 30th resolution, shall not delay the withdrawal of troops due to the delay in the organization and work of the team. (6) The next meeting of the Administrative Yuan is scheduled to be held on January 25, 1932. When necessary, the chairman may convene an emergency meeting at any time. (To be continued)

Tidbits 107

— Ping

The Shanghai war has given us the most profound stimulus. It is the violence displayed by the air force. Therefore, everyone feels that in the near future, China's "expansion of the air force" is something that can no longer be delayed. Although China's air force is very immature, I believe that if the Northeast planes had not been seized by the violent Japanese, and if the strength of the national air force had been concentrated to resist Japan, the enemy planes would not have been so rampant. The Shanghai area would not have been ravaged so tragically. Furthermore, how could there have been such an alarming loss of 140,000,000 yuan?

Recently, Director Zhang Hui visited Beijing. It is said that it is related to the issue of forming an air force. He has drafted a "Three-Year Air Force Plan," dividing it into three aviation zones: Beiping, Nanjing, and Guangzhou. It is expected that each zone will train 100 fighter planes in the first year, 300 in the second year, and 500 in the third year. Each zone will also set up a factory to manufacture engines. I hope that this great plan can be realized with the strength of the people of the whole country. The implementation of donating three planes per county and one plane per small county in Guangdong Province is especially hoped that the government will issue an order throughout the country and implement it on schedule. With the greatest determination, the greatest success will be achieved.

The Seven Women of the Skull Squad 108

— Shi Yan Ye

The Skull Squad comes from the north. Vowing to wipe out the barbarians, they do not wish to return alive. The squad has a total of more than eighty members. Upon arriving in Zhengyi, they joined under Commander Qu Shounian of the 19th Route Army. They earnestly requested to work on the front lines. Commander Qu was moved by their sincerity and agreed. Among the squad members are seven women, all young. They are beautiful in appearance and their clothing is extremely fashionable, truly so-called modern people. Commander Qu, pitying their weak and isolated nature, instructed them to serve in the rear, in order to reduce their hardship. The seven women said, "Commander's kindness is greatly appreciated, but we do not wish to accept it. Although we are women, we truly do not wish to be subordinate to men. We are also confident in our abilities, which are no less than those of men. Commander's move is discrimination against men and women. We have decided to go to the front with the male squad members and to share the same hardships with the male squad members. If one day our performance is not as good as the men's, then Commander may transfer us to the rear or even punish or execute us for poor performance. At that time, we will vow not to accept the order." Commander Qu was greatly moved upon hearing this and immediately granted their request. After the entire squad arrived at the front lines, they engaged in the construction of defensive works. The seven women worked with their own hands, regardless of wind or rain. Their physical strength and diligence were no less than those of the men. Their work performance was not only not inferior, but perhaps even exceeded it. The ladies slept in the sand every day and night. They had already dedicated themselves to the country, so they had no time to tidy up their clothes or wish to preserve their beauty. To this day, they all have bare heads and feet, and have exchanged their cheongsams for battle robes. The matter was reported to Shanghai yesterday by a gentleman who served on the front lines. When asked about the names of the ladies, he said that he did not know. It is truly a regrettable matter that they cannot be individually recognized.

Battlefield Photographs 109

— Ziwei

The violent Japanese invade, inhumanely. Zhabei and Wusong are a scene of ruins. The Mingxing Film Company has produced a film of the actual battlefield. Everything, from the cruel traces of the Japanese army to the suffering of our people, has been collected one by one, in great detail, without omission. When filming, Japanese planes followed and dropped bombs. In the end, they were able to overcome difficulties and dangers to make this great film. Its preciousness can be known. The National Government has ordered a copy to be sent to the League of Nations, in order to publicize the barbarity of the violent Japanese to the world. Cunning as the Japanese are, they will probably not be able to cover it up again.

At the beginning of the month, the League of Nations investigation commissioners visited Beijing. Zhang Shichuan and several technicians traveled to Nanjing. At the reception at the Lishi Society, they shot many sound films. On the way back, they passed through Wumen and stayed outside Jinchaomen. Through the introduction of Brigade Commander Weng, they specially went to Taicang, Kunshan, Qingyanggang and other places to film the military life of our 19th Route Army. All the commanders, including Cai Tingkai, were filmed.

The entire trip lasted two weeks. Every day they worked on the front lines. They have all returned to Shanghai, and their faces are dark and their beards are disheveled due to the wind and frost. It is said that when filming, enemy reconnaissance planes often came to the position and circled around. Our 19th Route Army stood ready, full of spirit. They did not slacken in the slightest in their defensive works. This can be used to comfort the people of the country. It is said that the sound film is already being printed. Those who are concerned about the front lines will soon be able to see our loyal and brave 19th Route Army again.

Shanghai War and Military Weapons (12) 110

— Yi Zang

In 1914, the World War broke out. The British army relied on tanks to win. However, at that time, they were only heavy vehicles of 15 to 20 tons, light vehicles of 5 to 10 tons, and 3-ton bean tanks for auxiliary use. With the development of technology, large tanks of 40 tons or more and 80 tons or less appeared. The armor ranged from 15 to 30 hao. The speed ranged from 30 to 50 kilometers. They were equipped with machine guns and light and heavy cannons. In the Battle of the Somme in 1916, the British army again relied on the power of tanks to repeatedly break through German positions. Thus, another epoch-making progress was made. Now, they have been changed to six-wheeled and tracked types. The maximum speed has reached 80 kilometers. They can be equipped with four machine guns. It is said that in the German army today, one battalion has 30 tanks. Last month, the United States invented a new amphibious light tank. The structure and equipment are even more exquisite. Because the tanks used in the past could only travel on land, and would sink when encountering loose, soft, or wet mud and sand, the amphibious vehicles can avoid all kinds of drawbacks.

Japanese tanks were manufactured after the World War, based on the British government's gift of female tanks as a standard. In recent years, the output has gradually increased. The ones sent to the Shanghai war this time are the country's only independent Kurume tank unit. They are all Japanese-made Type 89 tanks. They are equipped with Type 89 fighter planes. However, their armament, speed, and destructive power are also very strong. When fighting in Zhabei and Jiangwan, they were quite active in reconnaissance, combat, and heavy bombing. However, many of them were destroyed by our army's landmines. This point is also admitted by their Japanese newspapers.

Heroic Death (Middle) 111

— Mo Yi

A heroic and glorious battle began on the misty morning of the third day after the Old Zhao's team arrived in Jiangwan.

"Old Zhang, we've been here for two days, why haven't the short devils come? Why are they only attacking Zhabei? It's extremely hateful. Don't they want to try a new flavor? Are they looking down on us? Sigh, when we want them to come, they refuse to come. Could it be that Old Zhao's reputation has startled them? Haha, short devils, short devils, come on, what the hell are you waiting for!" Old Zhao said hatefully, smoking a cigarette.

"Old Zhao, stop chattering. Look, aren't they coming?" Old Zhang pulled Old Zhao's clothes, telling him to look at the line of things in the distance that looked the same crawling towards them in the dim light.

"What are those things? Old Zhang, they look like turtles." Old Zhao said, grabbing his cigarette and preparing his weapons, asking Old Zhang.

"Tanks." Old Zhang also aimed his gun at the enemy.

"How novel!... Ah, they're getting closer!... They're getting closer!"

When the officer gave the order to fire, the enemy's bullets were already flying over like raindrops. The enemy got closer and closer. Our brave warriors, without waiting for the officer's charge command, had already jumped out of the trenches and charged towards the enemy. How did these hot-blooded warriors make the enemy panic? Their bayonets, their bullets, their courage, their tactics, their actions, every performance of the battle, could threaten the enemy, letting them know that our warriors were so inviolable. The enemy could not help but retreat. The enemy could not help but find a safe place to protect their lives.

"Ha, the enemy has turned their backs on us! How satisfying, Old Zhang, we've really killed them to our heart's content today! Kill! Kill!... Kill!"

After a dense burst of gunfire and heroic shouts, dozens more enemies fell to the ground. After they repelled the enemy, they obeyed the officer's orders and returned to the trenches to defend. At this time, it was already bright. The sun still shone as usual, as if this cruel act on the earth had nothing to do with him.

"Old Zhang, you didn't lie to me. The short devils are indeed easier to fight than bandits! I've fought for eight years, and I've never fought so satisfyingly as today!"

Old Zhao shouted alone for a long time, but no one paid attention to him. He sulked in the trenches, looking at the clouds in the sky in a daze. The white smoke he exhaled from his mouth danced before his eyes, transforming into a symbol of killing even more satisfyingly than this time; the smile he held on his lips indicated that he had already obtained better and more satisfying tactics.

Commercial News

Financial: Last Week Gold Market Still Advancing 112

The market was very brisk in the first half of the week. Last week, the bidding gold price rose frequently. It was high from the beginning of the week, reaching a high price of 701.8 taels. Afterwards, the silver market repeatedly reported contractions, so it went forward bravely and a peak of 727 taels, the highest this year, appeared. However, there were ups and downs from time to time, but there were no special changes. The daily fluctuations were within 10 taels. By the weekend, it subsided again, probably because the current situation had an impact, and it retreated to the border of 710 taels. That day happened to be the rollover day. The short side posted it, first for 5 taels, then for 6.5 taels, and then for 4 taels, because the cash reserve was exhausted, so it was under pressure from all sides. In May, there was a review of 25.1 taels, and the total increase was 8.1 taels, so June was lower by 4 or 5 taels. The British-American exchange rate rose first and then fell, so the Shanghai market drafts were loose on the British side and tight on the American side. All the brokers bought and then sold. Now the British gold is slightly more bullish, while the American gold is still short-term. Most hedgers, if calculated according to the closing price of the American gold, deducted about 60 taels. Almost since the beginning of the week, several hundred bars of cash have been opened by the Central Bank, but later, because the price was not suitable, the industry was unwilling to sell it. Also, it was found that in recent days, there were many other star shorts in the exchange, as was the case with the Dalian gang, but the number of bars was limited, and spot firms and the Guangdong gang were all on the long side. Now, the past situation of the week is recorded again for reference.

A Sketch of the Entire Week's Process 113

Since Monday (April 11), the large gold bar still contracted 1.25, the American silver contracted 1.25, the first order was not changed, and the American gold increased by 1.25, because the exchange rate was high. The same was true for the domestic market. The industry bought near-term contracts. The gold price in May initially opened at 708.5 taels, then added 5.3 qian, followed by 0.9 taels. Afterwards, there were more sales, and it retreated to 0.2 taels, followed by fluctuations of 2 or 3 taels. It closed in the morning at 0.39 qian, and 0.4 taels in the afternoon. The market opened and then large households sold, starting at 0.18 qian. The Central Bank opened 400 or 500 bars of cash, and the price rose to 0.52 qian. When it closed, it retreated to 0.29 qian, a decrease of 3 qian from the previous Saturday. The entire day saw a fluctuation of 7.2 qian. The Dalian gang sold short positions, and the Guangdong gang and spot firms bought to offset the sold spots.

(Tuesday) Large gold bar and silver price each increased by 1.15, and the British and American exchange rates were stable. However, the industry was still relentlessly buying American gold. The gold market initially opened flat, slightly adding 1 qian, to 703 taels. Because there were buyers on the ground who were content, the market stabilized. Afterwards, it rotated upwards. Speculator Wu and large households bought, actually reaching 710 taels, at 12.5 taels. It closed in the morning at 0.92 qian. In the afternoon, it opened at 0.9 taels, followed by 10 taels, and then fluctuations of 1 or 2 taels. The Central Bank opened another 175 bars, but the sellers were not idle, and it retreated to 0.76 qian. When it closed, it was 0.87 qian, an increase of 5.8 qian from the previous day. The entire day saw an ebb and flow of 9.5 taels.

(Wednesday) British silver contracted 1.25, American silver contracted 0.25, the Shanghai market was flat on the British side and strong on the American side. Then, because the listing was changed to a smaller range, the first order was 0.25, and the American gold was 0.375, so the domestic market was also tight. Various firms struggled to buy, but Citibank sold. The bidding gold price initially opened and added 3.3 qian, to 712 taels, followed by 13.5 taels to 11.5 taels. Afterwards, as the exchange market tightened, it gradually rose, reaching 19.1 qian. It closed in the morning at 18.6 qian. The market opened in the afternoon at 18.8 qian. The buyers showed courage and broke through 20 taels, followed by a close at 23 taels, a continued increase of 14.3 qian from the previous day. The entire day saw a review of 11.5 taels. As the rollover day approached, the short side urgently covered.

(Thursday) Large gold bar contracted 1.875, American silver contracted 0.25, but the listing of the exchange market did not change. The domestic market was loose on the British side and firm on the American side. This was because the exchange rate was small. The gold market opened at 723 taels. However, the large gold bar contracted slightly too much. Fortunately, the ground was still good, and it was able to stabilize. Afterwards, large households excitedly competed to buy, and the American gold became even stronger, reaching a peak of 27 taels. However, Wu and various firms took the opportunity to sell, and the trend turned sharply downwards. It closed in the morning at 21.9 qian. In the afternoon, it was 21.5 qian. Afterwards, rumors spread, and it fell to 19.5 taels. Later, because the printed exchange rate was small, it saw a high rise. When it closed, it was 23.2 qian, an increase of only 2 qian from the previous day. The entire day saw a difference of 7.5 taels.

(Friday) The British and American silver markets each contracted 1.25, the first order increased 1.25, and the American gold also increased 1.25, so the exchange rate was slightly smaller and not affected. Also, according to the report on the ground, the United States had a saying about maintaining the silver price, so the domestic market was also loose. The gold market initially opened and decreased by 3.2 qian, to 720 taels. Later, Reuters reported that Germany had bought a large batch of cash silver to mint silver coins, totaling about 100 million marks, so the market went downstream and reduced more than 4 taels, to 15.8 qian. Later, it increased to 20.5 qian. It closed in the morning at 19.5 qian. In the afternoon, it was 18.8 qian. The market closed at 18 taels, a decrease of 5.2 qian from the previous day. The entire day saw 5.4 qian. The upward and downward situation was still flat.

(Saturday) Large gold bar increased 1.875, American silver increased 3.75, British and American exchange rates each increased 1.25, and the domestic market was also insufficient. As the bidding gold price coincided with the rollover day, there were no transactions in May. The opening price was 718 taels, and it closed at 11.3 qian. The first day of June opened at 712.5 taels, and then there were slight changes. It had reached 15.2 qian. At 11 o'clock, news of the tense situation between Japan and Russia and Japan and the United States was suddenly heard, and the market went down, dropping 8 taels. The situation suddenly deteriorated. It closed in the morning at 0.73 qian. However, there were not many transactions on the rollover day. In half a day, there was also a review of 7.9 qian. Tea Merchants Prepare Funds for Departure 115

As the Grain Rain solar term approaches, new tea from tea-producing areas is gradually appearing on the market. The main outlet depends on tea merchants in Shanghai for procurement. This year, due to the impact of the current situation on the financial sector, loans are not easily granted, causing tea merchants to hesitate. While they are trying to raise funds, the amount is ultimately limited and insufficient to meet the fixed amount for procurement. According to investigations, several reputable tea firms, such as Company A, B, and C, are raising funds through their own resources and financial accommodations to gather a large sum of cash for their scheduled departure to purchase tea. Other tea merchants are mostly waiting passively, hoping for assistance from various parties. It is said that due to fewer purchases this year, prices in the tea-producing regions have dropped sharply, making profits potentially attractive.

General Situation of Yarn and Cotton in Shanghai in March 120

Spot Yarn Prices Fall Sharply The cotton yarn market in March was relatively stable. Due to the suspension of operations by Japanese factories and the inability of Chinese factories to operate at full capacity, production significantly decreased, and market sentiment was somewhat firm. However, from the middle of the month, actual demand became extremely sluggish, and various groups showed no enthusiasm. The reasons for this are attributed to the financial exhaustion and transportation disruptions following the outbreak of the Shanghai War, as well as the severe impact of last year's floods. Moreover, the economic difficulties caused by the war in the inland areas are beyond description, all of which have dealt a significant blow to the yarn market. In previous years, there should have been a period of strong sales during the spring season, but the current situation is hopeless. As a result, morale has declined, and factories' inventories have increased daily, leading to a sharp decline in the market. The situation was particularly severe in the latter half of the month, with 42-count yarn falling by as much as 20 taels and 20-count yarn falling by over 10 taels. Coarse yarn saw less of a decline. Statistics show that actual sales this month were only 8,520 bales, with Guangdong accounting for the most at 2,447 bales, followed by Sichuan at 1,510 bales, Jiangxi at 583 bales, and inland areas at 631 bales. Other transactions were only sporadic. The volume of purchases by each group is listed below:

Grain and Rice Market: High Prices Initially, then Softening 121

South Shanghai: Yesterday, supplies from various groups continued to arrive, with a slight increase in inventory in Pudong, totaling about 80 companies, mostly "Guan Ju". North Shanghai: Yesterday, 30-40 cargoes arrived along the Suzhou River. Transactions on this street were sluggish, and the decline in prices was similar to that in the South Market. Kunshan and Jiangyin rice saw a shortage of 0.1 yuan, and top-quality goods were particularly scarce. The arrival of Suzhou and Changzhou "Bai Geng" was limited, and the opening prices were fixed. Silk and Tea: Silk Market Continues to Weaken 122

Overseas Markets See New Low Prices... Chinese Silk Merchants Face Difficulty Selling

The silk market, both domestic and international, was extremely weak last week. In New York, due to the boycott of Japanese goods, Japanese silk was aggressively sold at low prices, leading to new lows for both Chinese and Japanese silk, with prices falling by 0.2-0.45 US dollars per pound. In Lyon, spring sales of silk fabrics remained sluggish, inventories were high, and summer fabrics increasingly used rayon, significantly reducing the demand for raw silk. Furthermore, a large amount of Japanese silk was imported before the tax increase, resulting in strong inventories. Silk prices gradually declined, with both Chinese and Japanese silk falling by 4-5 francs per kilogram. In London, silk sales were sluggish, and printed silk for lower garments remained unsold. Due to the tense exchange rate with England, both Chinese and Japanese silk fell by 2-3 pence per pound. Shanghai's Chinese silk merchants hold inventory with high costs: white silk factories need to sell for over 1,000 taels, while overseas telegram prices for New York B-grade 80% evenness are less than 500 taels in Chinese silver, and London and Lyon AB-grade 13-15 filaments are only over 700 taels. Factories would lose 300-400 taels per bale, so they insist on not selling. Sales of Sichuan dry silk to Europe were also sluggish, while yellow and white coarse silk sales to India were not quiet. Only 300 bales of spot silk were transacted last week, with exports of just over 200 bales. The list of overseas market prices for Chinese silk at the end of last week is as follows:

Textiles 123

Spot Transactions Predominate in Woolen Fabrics

Woolen fabrics have been trading actively recently, with demand from various groups. However, large wholesale transactions remain limited. Sellers generally require spot transactions with tickets, otherwise they prefer not to sell. They are willing to make concessions on prices. In recent days, except for long-term customers, spot transactions are required for all quantities, whether half a bolt or a full bolt. As a result, street brokers find it difficult to solicit business, and buyers are also cautious, unlike previous years when they could arbitrarily allocate various goods.

Metals: New Arrivals of American Galvanized Iron 124

New shipments of American galvanized iron arrived yesterday, totaling several thousand "dan", further filling the Shanghai market. The market is under pressure from an unfavorable environment and continues to decline. Currently, 48-gauge is selling for 15.5 taels per "dan", 38-gauge for 15.6 taels, 33-gauge for 14.5 taels, and 25-gauge for 13.75 taels. It is reported that for large transactions, prices may be slightly cheaper. It is said that besides shipments of 40-50 "dan" by customer groups in recent days, there has been little interest from other groups.

Pig Lead Rebounds by 0.025 Taels 125

Yesterday, the price of pig lead rebounded because industry peers discussed ways to maintain prices due to cutthroat competition. Therefore, it was agreed to increase the price by 0.025 taels, to 14.25 taels per "dan". Transactions with tea merchants continued to be brisk, and businesses from Tianjin and Hankou also saw some activity. However, business on this street remained sluggish.

Local Supplement

Essays

Do Not Go to Zhabei 126

— Jin

The Ta Mei Wan Bao (Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury) reports, "The Chinese political organization under Japanese control in Zhabei, which appeared on April 1st, was dissolved by order of the Japanese naval authorities on April 11th, but reappeared today (16th). However, the leading figures are no longer the same."

Upon seeing this news, I took a deep breath of cold air. Although the old traitors have been disbanded, new puppets have emerged. I believe that this is the same old trick, just repeated. I initially wanted to pick up my pen and scold them thoroughly, but after thinking about it, I realized it was unnecessary, because there are so many traitors, they are beyond scolding. Moreover, since they are traitors, the national laws will punish them, and the universal principles of humanity will condemn them. These brainless, heartless creatures are only "three parts human, seven parts beast." It is not worth defiling my writing to harshly scold them.

Under the current circumstances, my proposal is a new slogan: "Do Not Go to Zhabei" in five big characters. Because ordinary people should not go to Zhabei. Once they go, they will inevitably be subjected to the commands, restrictions, extortion, and coercion of the traitors. I ask, are we, the good people, willing to be maintained and protected by a pack of foxes and dogs? Therefore, my saying "Do Not Go to Zhabei" means that I advise everyone:

Those who want to live, do not live in Zhabei. Those who want to do business, do not do business in Zhabei. Those who want to travel, do not travel in Zhabei.

In short, before the Japanese soldiers have completely withdrawn, do not go to Zhabei. Do not look at the hideous faces of the Japanese people. Do not look at the pretenses of the traitors. Food, clothing, housing, and transportation are the four essential elements of human life. Originally, the national character of "settling down and valuing one's native land" made it difficult for the people who were used to living in Zhabei to move easily. Fortunately, after this military disaster, houses and property were mostly destroyed by artillery fire, and 70-80% of the residents have already moved. Now, the area has become a region of ghosts crying, gods wailing, and jackals and wolves roaming. Going there would inevitably stir up emotions and send shivers down one's spine.

Another point is that most of the people living in Zhabei are living under someone else's roof, and very few own their own property. If one is going to live under someone else's roof anyway, why must one settle in Zhabei? This approach, I believe, is very appropriate. The purpose of their maintenance association is first to maintain the enemy, and second to maintain themselves. As for maintaining the local area, I am afraid that they will never be able to do that. Only "Do Not Go to Zhabei" is the best and most appropriate solution.

Popular Literature and Art

New Yuefu Poems on the Shanghai Disaster 127

— Meng Tiaoshe Owner

Presenting the Military Map

Presenting the military map, selling Spring Shen, who is that person? A close relative in the imperial harem. Once the military map is presented, military intelligence is leaked. Thirty days of effort are abandoned in a single day. The country is ashamed to have such a person. All our soldiers and civilians point fingers. Why is it that he was arrested more than a month ago, and we have not heard whether the crime has been determined? If the crime is truly undeniable, it must be punished by national law and military law. If the accusation is false, then the suspicions of the public should be dispelled as soon as possible. Alas, there are hundreds or thousands of people who betray the country, but why am I blamed for merely presenting a military map? Do you not see the general guarding Liaodong lost territory, yet still has a mighty army under his command?

Dancing Craze

Ten thousand lights flicker in the shadows on the mirror screen. Dew dampens the streets, a jade expanse. The curtains are raised in all twelve jade pavilions. Sounds of Ziyun melodies fly out. The wind blows the silk sleeves, ascending the silver stage. Dragon flutes and phoenix pipes resound like thunder. Countless figures embrace the moon, drifting like smoke. Following the sound, the clogs can tread thousands of times. Among them, there are many fairies on Penglai. Red gauze veils their skin, a mere foot away. The shattered homeland is not discussed. Life is only fit to die in a gentle land. After the single silk dance, champagne is poured. Wine-soaked words tease the flowers, but the flowers do not resent. The silver moon is about to set, but the revelry has not stopped. Butterflies dream, still not awake. The ashes of Kunming Pond stretch ten thousand fathoms deep. Why still revel on the flower pond with such a heart?

Popular Science

Advertising Lights 128

— Nai Wei

At dusk, on the bustling Nanjing Road, we can see red, green, vivid, and beautiful lights emanating from the windows on both sides, displaying graphic trademarks and store names, which are very dazzling. These advertising lights really attract attention.

This light is called "Neon-Sign Light" in English, and we can translate it as "Neon Light". It has been changed from the "Mercury Arc Lamp", so many people call it "Mercury Lamp". It has a very short history, just like a little baby who has not yet completed a season since birth, but it is so vividly cute that shop owners are willing to spend more money to invite it to live in the glass window all day long, attracting a group of buyers.

The mercury arc lamp, also called the Cooper-Hewitt Lamp, is named after its inventor. The manufacturing method of this lamp is to first take a glass tube and soften it in a smokeless fire, and slowly bend it into various patterns or characters, and install it on a black bottom plate. The bottom plate can be made of lead sheet or thin wood. The length of the glass tube is about two feet to four feet. The ordinary thickness is only 7 to 13 millimeters (Millimeter). The two bent openings are placed behind the bottom plate; then the opening at one end is sealed with a metal electrode, and the air in the tube is evacuated with an air pump, so that the tube becomes a vacuum tube (Vacuum Tube). Mercury vapor (Mercury Vapor) is put into the tube, and the unsealed tube opening can also be sealed with a metal electrode. The electricity is connected to the two electrodes at the tube opening, and the current will pass through the mercury vapor, and then emit beautiful light; the colors of the light are green, blue, and yellow, but no matter what, red light can never be emitted. If a tube made of quartz is used instead of a glass tube, it can be turned into a kind of ultraviolet rays (Ultra-violet rays), which is found in sunlight. It can make us healthy and can also disinfect and sterilize. Recently, artificial sun lamps used in hospitals, which can be rented or bought on the market, are of this type, but the form is a bit different.

Later, Sir William Ramsay, a British scientist, analyzed neon from the air, so he took some rarefied neon and put it in instead of mercury gas. After the current passed through, red light was emitted. The red light is emitted by itself, not like the red light emitted by ordinary red glass light bulbs. It has a special ability to pass through smoke and fog, so the lights on airplanes, signal lights on trains and ships, and lights in ocean lighthouses are reliable when using it. If some mercury vapor is mixed into the neon tube, purple and blue light will be emitted. Using a light taupe glass tube will result in a beautiful green light; during the day, we can see light taupe-colored empty glass tubes in the shop windows, and they will probably emit green light in the evening. Speaking of neon, it is a very rare thing, accounting for one ten-thousandth of the volume of air. That is, only one liter can be analyzed from 100,000 liters; therefore, its value is very expensive, and one liter costs more than one hundred dollars. Fortunately, neon lamps do not use much, only a sparse amount.

The electricity passing through the lamp tube must have extremely high voltage, and the longer the lamp tube, the greater the voltage is needed, that is, the applied voltage is directly proportional to the length of the lamp tube. Because the distance between the two electrodes is two feet to four feet, a normal voltage of 220 volts (Volt) will not make it emit light, at least 4,500 volts or more is needed. If we usually connect an advertising lamp to the power supply, we must connect a transformer in the middle to increase the voltage. The current it needs is very small, much less than the electric lights we usually use.

There is also a type that uses helium sealed in the tube, which can be called a helium lamp, which can emit beautiful golden light. It can be seen on the streets of New York, but in Shanghai, they are all red and green. Because helium is even rarer than neon, only two countries in the world can produce it, so the price is much more expensive than neon, and the United States prohibits its export.

The disadvantage of the above three types of advertising lights is that they require high-voltage electricity, so a small advertising lamp also requires a transformer, and the price is slightly lower than a large one, on the glass tube and neon raw materials.

Our old brother can draw out air and bend glass tubes, Shanghai has the Nian Hong Deng Company, etc. that can manufacture various neon advertising lights, which are very delicate, but unfortunately, the raw materials are all purchased from other countries.

Casual Talk

Copying the Eight Characters 129

— Hongshui

One night, I felt an unusual sense of dullness in the surrounding air—well, 'Let's take a stroll' is what my mind told me: Although it was already past nine o'clock, my wish was finally realized.

Stepping into Zhejiang Road and turning a corner, I arrived at Fourth Avenue: My heart was filled with the hope of relieving my boredom, and I opened my eyes to look around: food, clothing, entertainment, everything was displayed in a lively and bustling manner: it could truly be called a complete street.

In a corner of this street, a crowd of people was gathered, each with a look of terror on their faces; driven by curiosity, I carefully walked over to see what was happening.

There stood two foreign constables and one Chinese constable, all wearing black jackets, each with a pistol hanging from their waist. They were holding onto one of our compatriots who looked like a merchant—the merchant being searched, rummaged like an eagle catching a chick; he suddenly lost his composure and trembled all over! The foreign constable, seeing this expression, put on an iron face and muttered a string of foreign words, as if ordering the Chinese constable:

"Careful; be vigilant, don't let anything slip by."

The Chinese constable showed an even greater look of obeying orders and being loyal to his duty, moving his thick and long hands, ceaselessly searching the merchant from head to toe!

...The merchant, unable to bear this oppression, said painfully:

"Officer! I'm sorry, I only have five silver dollars on me, borrowed from my fellow villagers from ×× Road ×× Lane. Please don't search, I wouldn't dare hide contraband as a businessman. I'm really scared to be searched, thank you very much for letting me go!"

Before he could finish speaking, "Damn it! Don't move!" the Chinese constable shouted fiercely at the merchant, while taking out a shiny pistol from his pocket and waving it twice in front of the merchant's face, "Are you going to move?" At the same time, the two foreign constables who were issuing orders, simultaneously bestowed him with a slap on the ear, and the other with a foreign ham fist; and also spoke in Shanghai dialect:

"You bastard! You're being difficult, suspected of being a reactionary! Don't run..."

Thus, the Chinese constable, looking victorious, grabbed the merchant by the scruff of his neck as he trembled, and dragged him to the ×× Bureau, go, go, go.

East, West, South, North

Breakdown of Peace Talks – Bai Tao 130

—

Since the 19th Route Army withdrew from Wusong, Zhabei, and Jiangwan due to insufficient reinforcements, there has been the so-called ceasefire conference. The ceasefire conference has been going on for a month, and outsiders naturally don't know what exactly is being discussed there. These days, I've heard that because the Japanese are insisting on unreasonable demands, the situation is precarious, and there is a risk of the ceasefire conference breaking down. Since this news was announced in various newspapers, I have been hoping every day that it would break down. This is truly an abnormal thought. People are there enduring humiliation and making concessions, hoping for the success of the ceasefire conference, but I am here hoping for it to break down.

Regardless of whether it's abnormal or not, the newspaper seller Zhang San has earned a lot of copper coins from me because of this news. Originally, after the 19th Route Army withdrew, his career of selling sensational news extras plummeted. No matter how hard he shouted outside the door, I would ignore him. But these days, when he shouts: "Extra! Just published!" my heart suddenly starts pounding, filled with the hope of a breakdown, a breakdown! But after buying it and seeing, "Today's subcommittee meeting, tomorrow's subcommittee meeting," peace is nowhere in sight, and a breakdown is just as unattainable! I can't help but curse the damned Zhang San for tricking me again!
